-- DS: r_ds_iraction_general
-- Check if a specific test OID exists as a test action
SELECT *
FROM irac_test_action
WHERE program_id = '17024'      -- Quest campaign ID
  AND oid = '<TEST_OID_HERE>';

-- DS: iraction_sharded
-- DRAFT – based on vetted OID/campaign lookup query
SELECT action_id,
       oid,
       campaign_id,
       ircm_terms_id,
       payout_trace,
       sku,
       ircm_category_list_id,
       doe
FROM irac_action2
WHERE campaign_id = 17024
ORDER BY doe;
limit 200
